<script>
(function () {
  const video = document.getElementById('bgVideo');
  if (!video) return;

  video.muted = true;
  video.defaultMuted = true;
  video.playsInline = true;
  video.setAttribute('muted', '');
  video.setAttribute('playsinline', '');
  video.setAttribute('webkit-playsinline', '');

  const tryPlay = () => {
    const playPromise = video.play();
    if (playPromise && typeof playPromise.catch === 'function') {
      playPromise.catch(() => {
        document.documentElement.classList.add('video-paused');
      });
    }
  };

  video.addEventListener('playing', () => {
    document.documentElement.classList.remove('video-paused', 'video-error');
  });

  video.addEventListener('error', () => {
    document.documentElement.classList.add('video-error');
  });

  if (video.readyState >= 2) {
    tryPlay();
  } else {
    video.addEventListener('canplay', tryPlay, { once: true });
  }

  window.addEventListener('load', tryPlay, { once: true });
  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', () => {
    if (!document.hidden) tryPlay();
  });
  document.addEventListener('click', tryPlay, { once: true });
  document.addEventListener('touchstart', tryPlay, { once: true, passive: true });
})();
</script>

function escapeHtml(value) {
  return String(value ?? '')
    .replaceAll('&', '&amp;')
    .replaceAll('<', '&lt;')
    .replaceAll('>', '&gt;')
    .replaceAll('"', '&quot;')
    .replaceAll("'", '&#039;');
}

function stripZl(name) {
  return String(name || '').replace(/\s*ז[״"]ל\s*$/g, '').trim();
}

function wheatIcon(extraClass = "") {
  return `<svg class="wheat-icon ${extraClass}" viewBox="0 0 42 70" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false">
    <line x1="21" y1="66" x2="21" y2="28" stroke="#9d873b" stroke-width="1.8" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <ellipse cx="21" cy="16" rx="6.4" ry="13" fill="#c99b3d" opacity="0.82"/>
    <line x1="18" y1="9" x2="12" y2="4" stroke="#d8b868" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <line x1="21" y1="6" x2="21" y2="1" stroke="#d8b868" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <line x1="24" y1="9" x2="30" y2="4" stroke="#d8b868" stroke-width="1.2" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <line x1="17" y1="16" x2="9" y2="13" stroke="#b98b32" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <line x1="25" y1="16" x2="33" y2="13" stroke="#b98b32" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <line x1="17" y1="23" x2="11" y2="22" stroke="#a67a2d" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <line x1="25" y1="23" x2="31" y2="22" stroke="#a67a2d" stroke-width="1.1" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <path d="M21 52 Q11 44 8 36" stroke="#667345" stroke-width="1.7" fill="none" stroke-linecap="round"/>
    <path d="M21 42 Q31 33 34 25" stroke="#667345" stroke-width="1.7" fill="none" stroke-linecap="round"/>
  </svg>`;
}

const detailLabels = [
  ['community', 'יישוב'],
  ['age', 'גיל'],
  ['birthDate', 'תאריך לידה'],
  ['role', 'תפקיד / אפיון'],

  ['burialPlace', 'מקום קבורה']
];

heroCount.textContent = `${people.length} נשמות יקרות`;

function getPersonalPhoto(person) {
  /*
    Important: familyGroupPhoto is a shared group/couple image.
    It should NOT be used as the personal image for every member of the same family.
    Personal cards now use only the private image path from `photo`, for example:
    images/people-original/person-055.jpg
  */
  const personal = String(person.photo || '').trim();
  if (personal && !personal.includes('/family-groups/')) return personal;

  const display = String(person.displayPhoto || '').trim();
  const group = String(person.familyGroupPhoto || '').trim();
  if (display && display !== group && !display.includes('/family-groups/')) return display;

  return '';
}

function photoWithFallback(src, alt, fallbackSvg, extraAttrs = '') {
  return `
    <img src="${escapeHtml(src)}" alt="${escapeHtml(alt)}" ${extraAttrs}
      onerror="this.hidden=true; this.nextElementSibling.hidden=false; this.closest('.has-photo')?.classList.remove('has-photo');">
    <span class="image-fallback" hidden>${fallbackSvg}</span>`;
}

grid.innerHTML = people.map((person, index) => {
  const displayName = stripZl(person.name);
  const personalPhoto = getPersonalPhoto(person);
  const hasPhoto = Boolean(personalPhoto);
  const thumb = hasPhoto
    ? photoWithFallback(personalPhoto, person.displayPhotoAlt || person.name, wheatIcon(), 'loading="lazy"')
    : wheatIcon();
  const meta = [person.community, person.age ? `גיל ${person.age}` : ''].filter(Boolean)
    .map(item => `<span>${escapeHtml(item)}</span>`).join('');
  const role = person.role ? `<span class="card-role">${escapeHtml(person.role)}</span>` : '';
  const label = hasPhoto ? `<span class="photo-label">תמונה אישית</span>` : ``;
  return `
    <button type="button" class="name-card ${hasPhoto ? 'has-photo' : ''}" data-index="${index}" aria-label="פתיחת מידע נוסף על ${escapeHtml(displayName)}">
      <span class="thumb">${thumb}</span>
      <span class="name-stack">
        <span class="name-link">${escapeHtml(displayName)}</span>
        <span class="zayin">ז״ל</span>
        <span class="card-meta">${meta}</span>
        ${role}
        ${label}
      </span>
    </button>`;
}).join('');

function setBox(box, element, content, isList = false) {
  if (!content || (Array.isArray(content) && content.length === 0)) {
    box.hidden = true;
    element.innerHTML = '';
    return;
  }
  box.hidden = false;
  if (isList) {
    element.innerHTML = content.map(item => `<li>${escapeHtml(item)}</li>`).join('');
  } else {
    element.textContent = content;
  }
}

function openPerson(index) {
  const person = people[index];
  if (!person) return;

  lastFocused = document.activeElement;
  const displayName = stripZl(person.name);
  modalName.textContent = displayName;
  modalStatus.textContent = 'ז״ל';
  modalKicker.textContent = person.familyGroupTitle || person.community || 'דף זיכרון';
  modalLead.textContent = person.candleDatesLine || person.family || person.role || '';

  modalDetails.innerHTML = detailLabels
    .filter(([key]) => person[key] !== undefined && person[key] !== null && String(person[key]).trim() !== '')
    .map(([key, label]) => `
      <div class="detail-item">
        <span class="detail-label">${escapeHtml(label)}</span>
        <span class="detail-value">${escapeHtml(person[key])}</span>
      </div>`).join('');

  setBox(storyBox, modalStory, person.storySummaryClean || person.storySummary || '');
  setBox(relativesBox, modalRelatives, person.relativesLines || [], true);
  setBox(quoteBox, modalQuote, person.candleQuote || person.candleMemoryLine || '');

  if (person.related && person.related.length) {
    relatedBox.hidden = false;
    modalRelated.innerHTML = person.related.map(item => `<li>${escapeHtml(item)}</li>`).join('');
  } else {
    relatedBox.hidden = true;
    modalRelated.innerHTML = '';
  }

  const personalPhoto = getPersonalPhoto(person);
  if (personalPhoto) {
    modalMedia.innerHTML = photoWithFallback(
      personalPhoto,
      person.displayPhotoAlt || person.name || displayName,
      wheatIcon('modal-wheat')
    );
  } else {
    modalMedia.innerHTML = wheatIcon('modal-wheat');
  }

  modal.classList.add('is-open');
  modal.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'false');
  document.body.classList.add('modal-open');
  modalCard.focus();
}

function closePerson() {
  modal.classList.remove('is-open');
  modal.setAttribute('aria-hidden', 'true');
  document.body.classList.remove('modal-open');
  if (lastFocused && typeof lastFocused.focus === 'function') lastFocused.focus();
}

grid.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
  const card = event.target.closest('.name-card');
  if (!card) return;
  openPerson(Number(card.dataset.index));
});

modal.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
  if (event.target.matches('[data-close-modal]')) closePerson();
});

document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
  if (event.key === 'Escape' && modal.classList.contains('is-open')) closePerson();
});
</script>
</body>
</html>
